#' Populate the users table with data from grouped credentials (per-institute lists)

                    		
                  

                  

                    159
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    160

                    165

                    166

populate_users_table <- function(conn, grouped_credentials) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    173
                    !
                    
                      
  cat("Found grouped_credentials_file, populating users...\n")

                    		
                  

                  

                    174
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    175
                    
                    
                      
  # ---- Helpers ----

                    		
                  

                  

                    176
                    !
                    
                      
  nz_chr <- function(x) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    177
                    !
                    
                      
    if (is.null(x) || (is.character(x) && length(x) == 0)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    178
                    !
                    
                      
      return(NA_character_)

                    		
                  

                  

                    179
                    
                    
                      
    }

                    		
                  

                  

                    180
                    !
                    
                      
    as.character(x)

                    		
                  

                  

                    181
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    182
                    !
                    
                      
  is_missing_pw <- function(x) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    183
                    
                    
                      
    # Treat NULL, NA, "", or literal "NULL" as missing

                    		
                  

                  

                    184
                    !
                    
                      
    is.null(x) ||

                    		
                  

                  

                    185
                    !
                    
                      
      length(x) == 0 ||

                    		
                  

                  

                    186
                    !
                    
                      
      is.na(x) ||

                    		
                  

                  

                    187
                    !
                    
                      
      identical(x, "") ||

                    		
                  

                  

                    188
                    !
                    
                      
      (is.character(x) && toupper(x) == "NULL")

                    		
                  

                  

                    189
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    190
                    !
                    
                      
  nz_lgl <- function(x, default = FALSE) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    191
                    !
                    
                      
    if (is.null(x) || length(x) == 0 || is.na(x)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    192
                    !
                    
                      
      return(default)

                    		
                  

                  

                    193
                    
                    
                      
    }

                    		
                  

                  

                    194
                    !
                    
                      
    as.logical(x)

                    		
                  

                  

                    195
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    196
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    197
                    
                    
                      
  # ---- Build rows from all institutes ----

                    		
                  

                  

                    198
                    !
                    
                      
  user_institute_map <- data.frame(

                    		
                  

                  

                    199
                    !
                    
                      
    userid = character(0),

                    		
                  

                  

                    200
                    !
                    
                      
    institute = character(0),

                    		
                  

                  

                    201
                    !
                    
                      
    preset_password = character(0),

                    		
                  

                  

                    202
                    !
                    
                      
    admin = logical(0),

                    		
                  

                  

                    203
                    !
                    
                      
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE

                    		
                  

                  

                    204
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    205
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    206
                    !
                    
                      
  institutes <- names(grouped_credentials)

                    		
                  

                  

                    207
                    !
                    
                      
  for (institute in institutes) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    208
                    !
                    
                      
    users <- grouped_credentials[[institute]]

                    		
                  

                  

                    209
                    !
                    
                      
    if (is.null(users)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    210
                    !
                    
                      
      next

                    		
                  

                  

                    211
                    
                    
                      
    }

                    		
                  

                  

                    212
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    213
                    !
                    
                      
    for (u in users) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    214
                    !
                    
                      
      uid <- nz_chr(u$userid)

                    		
                  

                  

                    215
                    !
                    
                      
      if (is.na(uid) || uid == "") {

                    		
                  

                  

                    216
                    !
                    
                      
        next

                    		
                  

                  

                    217
                    
                    
                      
      }

                    		
                  

                  

                    218
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    219
                    !
                    
                      
      pw <- if (is_missing_pw(u$password)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    220
                    !
                    
                      
        NA_character_

                    		
                  

                  

                    221
                    
                    
                      
      } else {

                    		
                  

                  

                    222
                    !
                    
                      
        as.character(u$password)

                    		
                  

                  

                    223
                    
                    
                      
      }

                    		
                  

                  

                    224
                    !
                    
                      
      adm <- nz_lgl(u$admin, default = FALSE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    225
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    226
                    !
                    
                      
      user_institute_map <- rbind(

                    		
                  

                  

                    227
                    !
                    
                      
        user_institute_map,

                    		
                  

                  

                    228
                    !
                    
                      
        data.frame(

                    		
                  

                  

                    229
                    !
                    
                      
          userid = uid,

                    		
                  

                  

                    230
                    !
                    
                      
          institute = institute,

                    		
                  

                  

                    231
                    !
                    
                      
          preset_password = pw,

                    		
                  

                  

                    232
                    !
                    
                      
          admin = adm,

                    		
                  

                  

                    233
                    !
                    
                      
          stringsAsFactors = FALSE

                    		
                  

                  

                    234
                    
                    
                      
        )

                    		
                  

                  

                    235
                    
                    
                      
      )

                    		
                  

                  

                    236
                    
                    
                      
    }

                    		
                  

                  

                    237
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    238
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    239
                    !
                    
                      
  if (nrow(user_institute_map) == 0) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    240
                    !
                    
                      
    cat("No users found in config.\n")

                    		
                  

                  

                    241
                    !
                    
                      
    return(invisible(NULL))

                    		
                  

                  

                    242
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    243
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    244
                    !
                    
                      
  cat(

                    		
                  

                  

                    245

    "Found users from config:",

                    		
                  

                  

                    246
                    !
                    
                      
    paste(unique(user_institute_map$userid), collapse = ", "),

                    		
                  

                  

                    247
                    !
                    
                      
    "\n"

                    		
                  

                  

                    248
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    249
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    250
                    
                    
                      
  # ---- Prepare data for insertion ----

                    		
                  

                  

                    251
                    !
                    
                      
  user_data <- data.frame(

                    		
                  

                  

                    252
                    !
                    
                      
    userid = user_institute_map$userid,

                    		
                  

                  

                    253
                    !
                    
                      
    institute = user_institute_map$institute,

                    		
                  

                  

                    254
                    !
                    
                      
    password = ifelse(

                    		
                  

                  

                    255
                    !
                    
                      
      is.na(user_institute_map$preset_password),

                    		
                  

                  

                    256
                    !
                    
                      
      vapply(

                    		
                  

                  

                    257
                    !
                    
                      
        user_institute_map$userid,

                    		
                  

                  

                    258
                    !
                    
                      
        function(x) generate_password(),

                    		
                  

                  

                    259
                    !
                    
                      
        character(1)

                    		
                  

                  

                    260
                    
                    
                      
      ),

                    		
                  

                  

                    261
                    !
                    
                      
      user_institute_map$preset_password

                    		
                  

                  

                    262
                    
                    
                      
    ),

                    		
                  

                  

                    263
                    !
                    
                      
    admin = as.integer(user_institute_map$admin), # store as 0/1 (portable)

                    		
                  

                  

                    264
                    !
                    
                      
    pwd_retrieval_token = sapply(

                    		
                  

                  

                    265
                    !
                    
                      
      user_institute_map$userid,

                    		
                  

                  

                    266
                    !
                    
                      
      function(x) digest::digest(paste0(x, Sys.time(), runif(1)))

                    		
                  

                  

                    267
                    
                    
                      
    ),

                    		
                  

                  

                    268
                    !
                    
                      
    pwd_retrieved_timestamp = NA_character_,

                    		
                  

                  

                    269
                    !
                    
                      
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE

                    		
                  

                  

                    270
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    271
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    272
                    
                    
                      
  # ---- Insert ----

                    		
                  

                  

                    273
                    !
                    
                      
  DBI::dbWriteTable(conn, "passwords", user_data, append = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    274
                    !
                    
                      
  cat("Added", nrow(user_data), "users to the database\n")

                    		
                  

                  

                    275
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    276
                    
                    
                      
  # ---- Display summary ----

                    		
                  

                  

                    277
                    !
                    
                      
  cat("\nAdded users and their passwords:\n")

                    		
                  

                  

                    278
                    !
                    
                      
  for (i in seq_len(nrow(user_data))) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    279
                    !
                    
                      
    cat(

                    		
                  

                  

                    280
                    !
                    
                      
      "User:",

                    		
                  

                  

                    281
                    !
                    
                      
      user_data$userid[i],

                    		
                  

                  

                    282
                    !
                    
                      
      "Institute:",

                    		
                  

                  

                    283
                    !
                    
                      
      user_data$institute[i],

                    		
                  

                  

                    284
                    !
                    
                      
      "Password:",

                    !
                    
                      
      user_data$password[i],

                    		
                  

                  

                    286
                    !
                    
                      
      "Admin:",

                    		
                  

                  

                    287
                    !
                    
                      
      as.logical(user_data$admin[i]),

                    		
                  

                  

                    288
                    !
                    
                      
      "\n"

    )

#' Query annotations table by coordinates

query_annotations_db_by_coord <- function(conn, coord, cols) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    509
                    4x
                    
                      
  table <- tolower("annotations") # only one table for now

                    		
                  

                  

                    510
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    511
                    
                    
                      
  # 1) enforce exactly one coordinate (scalar, not vector/list, not NA)

                    4x

                    518

  # if (!is.character(coord)) stop("Coordinate must be character (TEXT).")

                    		
                  

                  

                    520

                    4x

#' Voting module UI

                    173
                    
                    
                      
#' Voting module server logic

                    		
                  

                  

                    174
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    175
                    
                    
                      
#' Handles the server-side logic for the mutation voting workflow.

                    		
                  

                  

                    176
                    
                    
                      
#' This includes:

                    		
                  

                  

                    177
                    
                    
                      
#' - Reactively loading mutation images and metadata

                    		
                  

                  

                    178
                    
                    
                      
#' - Capturing user input (agreement, observation, comment)

                    		
                  

                  

                    179
                    
                    
                      
#' - Writing votes to a tsv file and session data to a database

                    		
                  

                  

                    180
                    
                    
                      
#' - Advancing to the next voting item based on user interaction or trigger source

                    		
                  

                  

                    181
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    182
                    
                    
                      
#' The module is triggered when the `login_trigger` reactive becomes active

                    		
                  

                  

                    183
                    
                    
                      
#' and optionally by `get_mutation_trigger_source()` to load new voting tasks.

                    		
                  

                  

                    184
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    185
                    
                    
                      
#' Annotations are saved to the database connection provided in `db_pool`.

                    		
                  

                  

                    186
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    187
                    
                    
                      
#' @param id A string identifier for the module namespace.

                    		
                  

                  

                    188
                    
                    
                      
#' @param login_trigger A reactive expression that indicates when a user has logged in.

                    		
                  

                  

                    189
                    
                    
                      
#' @param db_pool A database pool object (e.g. SQLite or PostgreSQL) for writing annotations.

                    		
                  

                  

                    190
                    
                    
                      
#' @param get_mutation_trigger_source A reactive expression that signals a new mutation should be loaded.

                    		
                  

                  

                    191
                    
                    
                      
#' @param cfg App configuration

                    		
                  

                  

                    192
                    
                    
                      
#' @param tab_trigger Optional reactive that triggers when the voting tab is selected.

                    		
                  

                  

                    193
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    194
                    
                    
                      
#' @return None. Side effect only: registers reactive observers and UI updates.

                    		
                  

                  

                    195
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    196
                    
                    
                      
votingServer <- function(

                    		
                  

                  

                    197
                    
                    
                      
  id,

                    		
                  

                  

                    198
                    
                    
                      
  cfg,

                    		
                  

                  

                    199
                    
                    
                      
  login_trigger,

                    		
                  

                  

                    200
                    
                    
                      
  db_pool,

                    		
                  

                  

                    201
                    
                    
                      
  get_mutation_trigger_source,

                    		
                  

                  

                    202
                    
                    
                      
  tab_trigger = NULL

                    		
                  

                  

                    203
                    
                    
                      
) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    204
                    8x

                    205
                    
                    
                      
    # validate cfg cols using "validate_cols" function from db_utils.R

                    		
                  

                  

                    206
                    8x

                    207

    # Helper function to create the "done" tibble

                    8x

                    3x

                    3x

        ALT = "-",

    find_annotation_file <- function(user_info) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    194
                    !
                    
                      
      if (is.null(user_info)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    195
                    !

                    197

                    202

                    203

                    !

                    1
                    
                    
                      
#' Initialize environment for the application

                    		
                  

                  

                    2
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    3
                    
                    
                      
#' Sets up the app environment directory and the database.

                    		
                  

                  

                    4
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    5
                    
                    
                      
#' @param config_file_path Character. Path to the configuration file.

                    		
                  

                  

                    6
                    
                    
                      
#'    Default is app_env/config/config.yaml in the current working directory.

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    
                    
                      
#' @return List with paths to user_data directory, database file, and config file

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    
                    
                      
init_environment <- function(

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    
                    
                      
  config_file_path

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    
                    
                      
) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    
                    
                      
  # check if "IMGVOTER_BASE_DIR" is set, then set it as base directory

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    3x
                    
                      
  base_dir <- Sys.getenv("IMGVOTER_BASE_DIR", unset = getwd())

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    3x
                    
                      
  default_file_path <- file.path(

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    3x
                    
                      
    get_app_dir(),

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    3x
                    
                      
    "default_env",

                    		
                  

                  

                    18
                    3x
                    
                      
    "config",

                    		
                  

                  

                    19
                    3x
                    
                      
    "config.yaml"

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    21
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    22
                    3x
                    
                      
  if (config_file_path == default_file_path) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    23
                    3x
                    
                      
    config_dir <- file.path(base_dir, "app_env", "config")

                    		
                  

                  

                    24
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    25
                    3x
                    
                      
    if (!dir.exists(config_dir)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    !
                    
                      
      copy_dir_from_app(config_dir)

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    !
                    
                      
      config_file_path <- file.path(config_dir, "config.yaml")

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    
                    
                      
    }

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    3x
                    
                      
  cfg <- ShinyImgVoteR::load_config(config_file_path)

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    3x
                    
                      
  print("Configuration loaded:")

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    3x
                    
                      
  print(cfg)

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    3x
                    
                      
  Sys.setenv(

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    3x
                    
                      
    IMGVOTER_BASE_DIR = normalizePath(base_dir, mustWork = TRUE),

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    3x
                    
                      
    IMGVOTER_CONFIG_FILE_PATH = normalizePath(config_file_path, mustWork = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    39
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    40
                    
                    
                      
  # Set up expected directories

                    		
                  

                  

                    41
                    3x
                    
                      
  expected_dirs <- c("images", "user_data", "server_data")

                    		
                  

                  

                    42
                    
                    
                      
  # browser()

                    		
                  

                  

                    43
                    3x
                    
                      
  purrr::walk(expected_dirs, function(name) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    44
                    9x
                    
                      
    key <- glue::glue("{name}_dir")

                    		
                  

                  

                    45
                    9x
                    
                      
    cfg_path <- cfg[[key]]

                    		
                  

                  

                    46
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    47
                    
                    
                      
    # Determine if path is relative or absolute

                    		
                  

                  

                    48
                    9x
                    
                      
    is_relative <- !grepl("^(/|[A-Za-z]:)", cfg_path) # Unix or Windows absolute path

                    		
                  

                  

                    49

leaderboardServer <- function(id, cfg, login_trigger, tab_trigger = NULL) {

overwrite_if_relative <- function(path) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    186x
                    
                      
  print(paste0("Checking if path is relative: ", path))

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    186x
                    
                      
  base_dir <- Sys.getenv("IMGVOTER_BASE_DIR")

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    186x
                    
                      
  is_relative <- !grepl("^(/|[A-Za-z]:)", path) # Unix or Windows absolute path

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    186x
                    
                      
  if (is_relative) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    146x
                    
                      
    print(paste0("Path is relative: ", path))

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    146x
                    
                      
    rel_path <- path

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    146x
                    
                      
    path <- normalizePath(file.path(base_dir, rel_path), mustWork = FALSE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    146x
                    
                      
    print(paste0("Overwriting with absolute path: ", path))

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    186x
                    
                      
  return(path)

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    
                    
                      
}

#' Create a Directory Safely

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    
                    
                      
#' Validates that the target directory name is a single word (letters, digits, and/or underscores only)

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
#' before attempting to create it. Optionally handles nested creation, warnings, and permission bits.

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    
                    
                      
#' @param path Character. The name (or path) of the directory to create.

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    
                    
                      
#'        Only the final component (basename) is validated.

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    
                    
                      
#' @param pattern Character. A regular expression that the directory name must match.

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    
                    
                      
#'        Default is `"^[A-Za-z0-9_]+$"`, i.e. one or more letters, digits, or underscores.

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    
                    
                      
#' @param showWarnings Logical. If `TRUE`, warns when the directory already exists or cannot be created.

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    
                    
                      
#'        Default is `TRUE`.

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    
                    
                      
#' @param recursive Logical. If `TRUE`, creates any missing parent directories (like `mkdir -p`). Default is `FALSE`.

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    
                    
                      
#' @param mode Character or numeric. Directory permissions in octal (e.g. `"0777"`). Default is `"0777"`.

                    		
                  

                  

                    39
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    40
                    
                    
                      
#' @return Invisibly returns `TRUE` if the directory was successfully created, `FALSE` otherwise.

                    		
                  

                  

                    41
                    
                    
                      
#'         If the directory already exists, returns `FALSE` (with a message, unless `showWarnings = FALSE`).

                    		
                  

                  

                    42
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    43
                    
                    
                      
#' @examples

                    		
                  

                  

                    44
                    
                    
                      
#' # Successful creation

                    		
                  

                  

                    45
                    
                    
                      
#' safe_dir_create("data_folder")

                    		
                  

                  

                    46
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    47
                    
                    
                      
#' # Fails validation (contains spaces)

                    		
                  

                  

                    48
                    
                    
                      
#' try(safe_dir_create("my data"))

                    		
                  

                  

                    49
                    
                    
                      
safe_dir_create <- function(

                    		
                  

                  

                    50
                    
                    
                      
  path,

                    		
                  

                  

                    51
                    
                    
                      
  pattern = "^[A-Za-z0-9_]+$",

                    		
                  

                  

                    52
                    
                    
                      
  showWarnings = TRUE,

                    		
                  

                  

                    53
                    
                    
                      
  recursive = FALSE

                    		
                  

                  

                    54
                    
                    
                      
) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    55
                    6x
                    
                      
  name <- basename(path)

                    		
                  

                  

                    56
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    57
                    
                    
                      
  # Validate against the pattern

                    		
                  

                  

                    58
                    6x
                    
                      
  if (!grepl(pattern, name)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    59
                    !
                    
                      
    stop(

                    		
                  

                  

                    60
                    !
                    
                      
      "Invalid directory name: '",

                    		
                  

                  

                    61
                    !
                    
                      
      name,

                    		
                  

                  

                    62
                    !
                    
                      
      "'. Only letters, digits and underscores are allowed."

                    		
                  

                  

                    63
                    
                    
                      
    )

                    		
                  

                  

                    64
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    65
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    66
                    
                    
                      
  # If it already exists, warn or message and return FALSE

                    		
                  

                  

                    67
                    6x
                    
                      
  if (dir.exists(path)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    68
                    6x
                    
                      
    if (showWarnings) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    69
                    6x
                    
                      
      message("Directory '", path, "' already exists.")

                    		
                  

                  

                    70
                    
                    
                      
    }

                    		
                  

                  

                    71
                    6x
                    
                      
    return(invisible(FALSE))

                    		
                  

                  

                    72
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    73
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    74
                    
                    
                      
  # Create the directory

                    		
                  

                  

                    75
                    !
                    
                      
  dir.create(

                    		
                  

                  

                    76
                    !
                    
                      
    path,

                    		
                  

                  

                    77
                    !
                    
                      
    showWarnings = showWarnings,

                    		
                  

                  

                    78
                    !
                    
                      
    recursive = recursive

                    		
                  

                  

                    79
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    80
                    
                    
                      
}

                    		
                  

                  

                    81
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    82
                    
                    
                      
# Ensure that .gitignore in dir contains the given patterns

                    		
                  

                  

                    83
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    84
                    
                    
                      
#' This function checks if a .gitignore file exists in the specified directory.

                    		
                  

                  

                    85
                    
                    
                      
#' If it does not exist, it creates one. It then ensures that the specified patterns

                    		
                  

                  

                    86
                    
                    
                      
#' are present in the .gitignore file, adding them if they are missing.

                    		
                  

                  

                    87
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    88
                    
                    
                      
#' @keywords internal

                    		
                  

                  

                    89
                    
                    
                      
#' @param dir Character. Directory path where the .gitignore file should be checked/created.

                    		
                  

                  

                    90
                    
                    
                      
#' @param patterns Character vector. Patterns to ensure in the .gitignore file.

                    		
                  

                  

                    91
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    92
                    
                    
                      
#' @return Character path to the .gitignore file

                    		
                  

                  

                    93
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    94
                    
                    
                      
ensure_gitignore <- function(directory, patterns) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    95
                    3x
                    
                      
  dir_full_path <- normalizePath(directory, mustWork = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    96

pending_logout_tasks <- new.env(parent = emptyenv())

#' @keywords internal

                    		
                  

                  

                    9

schedule_logout_update <- function(sessionid, callback, delay = 5) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    2x
                    
                      
  cancel_pending_logout(sessionid)

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    2x
                    
                      
  handle <- later::later(

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    2x
                    
                      
    function() {

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    1x
                    
                      
      callback()

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    1x
                    
                      
      rm(list = sessionid, envir = pending_logout_tasks)

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    
                    
                      
    },

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    2x
                    
                      
    delay

                    		
                  

                  

                    18
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    19
                    2x
                    
                      
  assign(sessionid, handle, envir = pending_logout_tasks)

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    
                    
                      
}

#' @keywords internal

cancel_pending_logout <- function(sessionid) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    4x

                    28
                    1x
                    
                      
    handle()

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    1x
                    
                      
    rm(list = sessionid, envir = pending_logout_tasks)

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    
                    
                      
}

# coalescing operator: return `a` if it exists and is non-empty,

                    		
                  

                  

                    2
                    
                    
                      
# otherwise fall back to `b`.

                    		
                  

                  

                    3
                    
                    
                      
`%||%` <- function(a, b) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    4
                    
                    
                      
  # If `a` is NULL, there is nothing to return

                    		
                  

                  

                    5
                    !
                    
                      
  if (is.null(a)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    6
                    !
                    
                      
    return(b)

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    
                    
                      
  # If `a` is a character but empty ("") or all whitespace, also use `b`

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    !
                    
                      
  if (is.character(a) && !nzchar(a)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    !
                    
                      
    return(b)

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    
                    
                      
  # Otherwise keep the original value

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    !
                    
                      
  a

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    
                    
                      
}

#' Build base URL from session data, accounting for reverse proxy subpaths

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    21
                    
                    
                      
#' @param session Shiny session object

                    		
                  

                  

                    22
                    
                    
                      
#' @return Complete base URL including protocol, host, port, and pathname

                    		
                  

                  

                    23
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    24
                    
                    
                      
build_base_url <- function(session) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    25
                    
                    
                      
  # 1) Protocol from the browser, not guessed from port

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    !
                    
                      
  proto_raw <- session$clientData$url_protocol %||% "https:"

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    !
                    
                      
  proto <- sub(":$", "", tolower(proto_raw)) # "http:" -> "http"

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
  # 2) Hostname

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    !
                    
                      
  host <- session$clientData$url_hostname %||% "localhost"

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    
                    
                      
  # 3) Port: include only if present and non-default for the protocol

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    !
                    
                      
  port_val <- session$clientData$url_port

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    !
                    
                      
  port_part <- ""

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    !
                    
                      
  if (!is.null(port_val) && nzchar(as.character(port_val))) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    !
                    
                      
    port_num <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(port_val))

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    !
                    
                      
    is_default <- (proto == "http" && identical(port_num, 80L)) ||

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    !
                    
                      
      (proto == "https" && identical(port_num, 443L))

                    		
                  

                  

                    39
                    !
                    
                      
    if (!is_default) port_part <- paste0(":", port_val)

                    		
                  

                  

                    40
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    41
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    42
                    
                    
                      
  # 4) Pathname: keep subpath, drop query, normalize trailing slash

                    		
                  

                  

                    43
                    !
                    
                      
  pathname <- session$clientData$url_pathname %||% "/"

                    		
                  

                  

                    44
                    !
                    
                      
  pathname <- sub("\\?.*$", "", pathname)

                    		
                  

                  

                    45
                    !
                    
                      
  if (!nzchar(pathname)) pathname <- "/"

                    		
                  

                  

                    46
                    !
                    
                      
  if (!grepl("/$", pathname)) pathname <- paste0(pathname, "/")

                    		
                  

                  

                    47
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    48
                    !
                    
                      
  paste0(proto, "://", host, port_part, pathname)

                    		
                  

                  

                    49
                    
                    
                      
}
